### No. 44: Cinematic Portrait with Strict Identity Preservation

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An image generation prompt designed for Nano Banana Pro to create a dreamlike, cinematic, ultra-realistic portrait of a woman. The prompt includes detailed specifications for style, lighting (warm amber natural sunlight), wardrobe (oversized white knitted shirt), and environment (neutral cream wall). Crucially, it mandates strict identity preservation, ensuring the face from a reference image is 100% maintained.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "type": "image_generation_prompt",
  "style": "dreamlike, cinematic, ultra-realistic portrait",
  "identity_preservation": {
    "use_reference_image": true,
    "alter_face": false,
    "strict_identity_lock": true,
    "notes": "Do not change the face in any way. Preserve 100% of the facial features, structure, skin texture, and likeness from the uploaded image."
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "female",
    "pose": {
      "head_position": "gently lowered",
      "expression": "calm, introspective, serene",
      "body_language": "relaxed and natural"
    },
    "appearance": {
      "hair": {
        "color": "black",
        "style": "tousled, natural movement"
      },
      "accessories": [
        "sunglasses creating a cool, effortless aura",
        "single thin silver necklace"
      ]
    }
  },
  "wardrobe": {
    "top": "white oversized knitted shirt made of soft, textured fabric"
  },
  "environment": {
    "background": {
      "color": "neutral cream wall",
      "style": "minimalist and clean"
    }
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "natural sunlight",
    "tone": "warm amber",
    "effects": [
      "soft glow brushing the face and shoulder",
      "cinematic warmth against the neutral background",
      "gentle highlights with smooth falloff"
    ]
  },
  "mood": {
    "atmosphere": "dreamlike, cinematic, peaceful",
    "emotion": "soft confidence and quiet elegance"
  },
  "quality": {
    "realism": "ultra-realistic",
    "detail_level": "high detail in skin texture, fabric weave, and lighting transitions"
  },
  "output_goal": "Create a dreamlike, cinematic portrait of a young woman wearing an oversized white knitted shirt, bathed in warm amber sunlight against a cream wall, while preserving her face exactly as in the reference image."
}
```

### No. 45: Grunge Sports Poster Portrait from Reference Image

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt for generating a dynamic, grunge-style sports poster portrait based on an uploaded image. It requires the subject to be shirtless, muscular, and in an intense profile pose, applying heavy impasto texture, chaotic paint splatters, and a split background of crimson red and charcoal black.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Dynamic grunge-style sports poster portrait of a [uploaded image] in celebration, intense profile pose looking directly at the camera. Shirtless with dark messy hair, showcasing an extremely defined muscular physique with strong vascularity. Use my reference image, keep my face 100% unchanged. Heavy impasto texture, bold palette knife strokes, chaotic paint splatters, gritty grunge overlays. Vertical split background: crimson red left, charcoal black center. vibrant golden yellow.
```

### No. 47: Identity-Locked Coquette Mirror Selfie

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed, structured prompt for Nano Banana Pro focusing on strict identity locking to generate a mirror selfie of a young woman with a warm, genuine smile and coquette aesthetic, holding a red tulip bouquet.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "reference": {
    "source_image": "uploaded_reference_image",
    "identity_lock": true,
    "strict_face_match": true,
    "face_preservation": "100% identical to the uploaded reference: no changes to facial structure, eyes, nose, lips, brows, skin tone, skin texture, proportions",
    "keep_unique_features": true,
    "no_identity_drift": true
  },

  "subject": {
    "type": "young_adult_woman",
    "ethnicity": "same_as_reference",
    "age": "adult_same_as_reference",
    "eye_color": "same_as_reference",
    "skin_texture": "same_as_reference_natural_with_visible_pores_and_imperfections_no_blur_or_smoothing",
    "expression": "warm_genuine_smile_with_soft_coquette_vibe",

    "makeup": {
      "finish": "matte",
      "blush": "light_pink",
      "eyeshadow": "soft_pink",
      "eyeliner": "thin_black",
      "lashes": "defined",
      "lip_color": "matte_dusty_pink",
      "lip_shape": "same_as_reference"
    },

    "hair": {
      "color": "same_as_reference",
      "length": "same_as_reference",
      "texture": "voluminous_defined_curls_glossy",
      "bangs": "same_as_reference_or_keep_visible_match",
      "crown_style": "natural_curl_volume_at_crown_no_braided_crown",
      "side_sections": "curly_face_framing_sections",
      "accessories": []
    },

    "nails": {
      "style": "short_coquette",
      "color": "pastel_pink"
    },

    "pose": {
      "type": "mirror_selfie",
      "camera_angle": "slight_downward_diagonal",
      "head_angle": "very_subtle_tilt",
      "body_position": "leaning_forward_slightly",
      "right_arm": "holding_phone",
      "left_arm": "holding_red_tulip_bouquet_close_to_torso"
    }
  },

  "apparel": {
    "top": {
      "type": "red_crop_top",
      "pattern": "solid",
      "fit": "tight_and_form_fitting",
      "closure": "secure_no_gapping",
      "neckline": "tasteful_covered_no_cleavage_focus",
      "sleeves": "optional_short_or_long_sleeves",
      "integrity": "top_stays_in_place_no_sliding_no_opening",
      "opacity": "fully_opaque_non_see_through"
    },

    "undershirt": {
      "type": "none",
      "material": "n/a",
      "coverage": "top_is_opaque_non_see_through"
    },

    "necklace": {
      "type": "minimalist_silver_chain",
      "pendant": "tiny_simple_shape"
    },

    "bottoms": {
      "type": "red_mini_skirt",
      "details": "opaque_non_see_through_clean_seams"
    }
  },

  "phone": {
    "model": "iPhone_15_Pro_Max",
    "held_in": "right_hand",
    "case": {
      "design": "solid_red_case",
      "details": {
        "finish": "matte_or_soft_gloss",
        "edges": "clean_minimal"
      },
      "inserted_photo": "none"
    }
  },

  "environment": {
    "setting": "modern_warm_cozy_home_interior",
    "walls": {
      "color": "warm_neutral_tone",
      "decor": {
        "posters": [],
        "garlands": "none_or_subtle"
      }
    },

    "bed": {
      "sheets": "neutral_or_soft_pastel",
      "pillows": "neutral_or_soft_pastel"
    }
  }
}
```

### No. 48: Hyper-Realistic Tropical Transformation with Face Lock

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed JSON prompt for Nano Banana Pro, designed for hyper-realistic image editing. The core intent is to transform the subject's body, outfit, and environment into a premium tropical aesthetic (secluded beach cove, sunset lighting) while maintaining the reference face with absolute accuracy and zero identity drift. It specifies Korean-inspired wavy hair, a low-cut halter top, and a high-slit sarong skirt.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "model": "image_editing_pro",
  "task": "hyper_realistic_face_preserved_edit",
  "core_intent": "Transform body, outfit, and environment into a premium tropical aesthetic while maintaining the reference face with absolute accuracy and zero identity drift.",
  "reference_handling": {
    "source_face": "attached_image",
    "face_lock": true,
    "identity_protection_level": "maximum",
    "allowed_changes": "none_on_face"
  },
  "subject_design": {
    "appearance": "young woman with fair natural skin and long Korean-inspired wavy hair in a soft brown-blonde shade, styled into a loose, thick braid",
    "hair_details": "braid decorated with a large light-purple orchid clip and delicate white flowers subtly woven throughout for an elegant tropical touch"
  },
  "wardrobe_styling": {
    "top": "low-cut halter top in silky fabric with subtle lace accents and thin straps that accentuate the shoulders",
    "bottom": "high-slit sarong skirt in sheer chiffon, revealing toned legs with a hint of mystery",
    "arm_accessories": "delicate gold chain armlets that drape elegantly, adding a touch of allure"
  },
  "pose_and_expression": {
    "body_language": "leaning forward slightly with hand on hip, exuding confident sultriness",
    "facial_expression": "mysterious half-smile with sultry, inviting gaze identical to the reference's emotional identity"
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "secluded tropical beach cove",
    "background_elements": "gentle waves lapping at golden sand, surrounded by lush palm fronds",
    "sky": "vibrant sunset with deep oranges and purples, casting a warm, intimate glow"
  },
  "lighting_design": {
    "type": "authentic tropical sunlight",
    "characteristics": "realistic highlights, dynamic yet soft shadows, accurate skin reflections without artificial glow",
    "contrast_balance": "natural high contrast with smooth tonal transitions"
  },
  "visual_style": {
    "rendering": "ultra-hyperrealistic",
    "skin_texture": "true-to-life, visible fine details without filters",
    "color_theme": "deep oranges, purples, golds, and warm skin tones",
    "overall_mood": "romantic, tropical, premium, sultry and elegant"
  },
  "camera_setup": {
    "lens": "85mm portrait",
    "angle": "eye-level",
    "depth_of_field": "shallow with creamy background blur",
    "composition": "large foreground subject dominance"
  },
  "technical_specs": {
    "resolution": "8K",
    "detail_level": "extreme fine detail",
    "quality": "maximum realism",
    "aspect_ratio": "3:2"
  },
  "restrictions": {
    "face_editing": "strictly forbidden",
    "beauty_filters": "disabled",
    "ai_face_reconstruction": "not_allowed"
  },
  "final_goal": "Create a visually striking tropical portrait where the reference face remains 100% unchanged, while the body styling and environment deliver a high-end, editorial-quality transformation.",
  "signature": "@siennalovesai"
}
```

### No. 52: 90s Yearbook Grid Collage

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt for Nano Banana Pro to transform a photo into a 3x3 grid collage mimicking vintage 1990s American yearbook portraits, complete with Olan Mills studio aesthetic, awkward poses, and specific film grain effects.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A 3x3 grid collage of 9 distinct, awkwardly posed vintage 1990s American yearbook portraits.

**Layout & Subjects:**

* **Center Panel (Row 2, Column 2):** Contains the main subject: [use the person in the attached photo as a late teenager], with a deer-in-headlights look wearing a very loud, geometrically patterned "ugly" knit sweater in clashing colors (purple, green, orange, blue) layered over a white collared shirt.

* **Surrounding 8 Panels:** Fill with diverse classmates featuring comically awkward expressions and exaggerated 90s styles:
    * **Top Row:** A girl with a massive, frizzy perm and thick glasses grinning goofily; a guy with a huge, feathered mullet in a denim jacket looking uncomfortable; a girl with a severe bowl cut and a strained, toothy smile.
    * **Middle Row (Left/Right):** A guy with a tall flat-top haircut giving a cheesy thumbs-up; another guy with a severe center part and a confused, open-mouthed stare.
      * **Bottom Row:** A girl with wildly crimped hair and a pained grimace; a guy wearing large, thick-rimmed tortoise-shell glasses, textured pastel knit crewneck sweater layered over a white collared shirt has a polite, slightly awkward smile; another girl with huge, teased bangs and a forced, tight-lipped grin.
**Style & Tech:**
Classic "Olan Mills" studio aesthetic applied uniformly to all 9 panels. All backgrounds are the generic mottled blue hand-painted canvas. Lighting is flat, broad studio flash with subtle rim lighting. Image quality features soft focus, heavy film grain, warm Kodak Gold 200 color grading, and a soft vignette over each individual panel.
```

### No. 55: Hyper-Realistic Tropical Portrait with Face Preservation

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured prompt for image editing, instructing the model to transform the body, outfit, and environment into a premium tropical aesthetic while strictly maintaining the identity and features of an uploaded reference face. It details wardrobe, lighting, and camera setup for an ultra-hyperrealistic result.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "model": "image_editing_pro",
  "task": "hyper_realistic_face_preserved_edit",
  "core_intent": "Transform body, outfit, and environment into a premium tropical aesthetic while maintaining the reference face with absolute accuracy and zero identity drift.",
  "reference_handling": {
    "source_face": "attached_image",
    "face_lock": true,
    "identity_protection_level": "maximum",
    "allowed_changes": "none_on_face"
  },
  "subject_design": {
    "appearance": "young woman with fair natural skin and long Korean-inspired wavy hair in a soft brown-blonde shade, styled into a loose, thick braid",
    "hair_details": "braid decorated with a large light-purple orchid clip and delicate white flowers subtly woven throughout for an elegant tropical touch"
  },
  "wardrobe_styling": {
    "top": "halter-neck swimsuit top in silk-like fabric with intricate seashell beadwork and soft fringe details",
    "bottom": "matching high-cut bottoms with side ties, layered under a translucent chiffon wrap skirt in pastel yellows",
    "arm_accessories": "woven vine bracelets adorned with tiny tropical blooms and pearl drops for a whimsical island charm"
  },
  "pose_and_expression": {
    "body_language": "seated elegantly on a hammock, with a relaxed yet poised demeanor",
    "facial_expression": "soft natural smile identical to the reference, calm eyes with untouched emotional identity"
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "secluded tropical hammock area",
    "background_elements": "swaying palm trees overhead, soft sand floor with scattered petals, distant view of lagoon",
    "sky": "golden hour glow with hues of amber and soft purple, creating a dreamy twilight ambiance"
  },
  "lighting_design": {
    "type": "authentic tropical sunlight",
    "characteristics": "realistic highlights, dynamic yet soft shadows, accurate skin reflections without artificial glow",
    "contrast_balance": "natural high contrast with smooth tonal transitions"
  },
  "visual_style": {
    "rendering": "ultra-hyperrealistic",
    "skin_texture": "true-to-life, visible fine details without filters",
    "color_theme": "pastel yellows, soft purples, greens, and warm amber tones",
    "overall_mood": "romantic, tropical, premium, subtly sexy but elegant"
  },
  "camera_setup": {
    "lens": "85mm portrait",
    "angle": "eye-level",
    "depth_of_field": "shallow with creamy background blur",
    "composition": "large foreground subject dominance"
  },
  "technical_specs": {
    "resolution": "8K",
    "detail_level": "extreme fine detail",
    "quality": "maximum realism",
    "aspect_ratio": "3:2"
  },
  "restrictions": {
    "face_editing": "strictly forbidden",
    "beauty_filters": "disabled",
    "ai_face_reconstruction": "not_allowed"
  },
  "final_goal": "Create a visually striking tropical portrait where the reference face remains 100% unchanged, while the body styling and environment deliver a high-end, editor"
```

### No. 56: Product Photography Grid Generation for Cost Saving

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

This prompt provides three variations for generating product photography grids using Nano Banana Pro. The goal is to quickly experiment with different moods, aesthetics, and product variations (or variations of the same product) in a 6x6 grid format to save credits on individual image generation.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Generate a 6x6 grid of professional product photography. Reference the original image's mood, quality, and aesthetic. Each cell should showcase a completely different product ({argument name="products" default="bags, bottles, hats, cosmetics, jewelry, food, electronics, etc."}) in a unique studio setting with a distinct color palette. Maintain the same high-end commercial photography style throughout. Vary the products, lighting, backgrounds, props, and styling dramatically across all 36 images.

Generate a 6x6 grid of variations based on the original image. Keep the same product but vary the color palettes, backgrounds, lighting, angles, props, and styling dramatically across all 36 cells. Maintain the same professional quality and aesthetic throughout.

Generate a 6x6 grid showing 36 unique variations of this product. Experiment wildly with color palettes, environments (studio, lifestyle, minimal, textured backgrounds), lighting styles, compositions, and moods. Keep product recognition and professional quality consistent, but make each cell visually distinct.
```

### No. 57: 2x2 Grid of Cocktails as Tiny Living Cities

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A creative food art prompt for Nano Banana Pro, generating a 2x2 grid of ultra-realistic macro cocktail photographs where each cocktail (Manhattan, PiÃ±a Colada, Negroni, Old Fashioned) is re-imagined as a tiny living city, detailing specific elements for each drink's cityscape.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A 2x2 grid of cocktails as tiny living cities
[Top Left: Manhattan; cherry wood skyline, tiny yellow cabs on vermouth river, glowing Luxardo cherry sun]
[Top Right: PiÃ±a Colada; pineapple wedge island with tiny rum distilleries, coconut palm elevators, creamy waves]
[Bottom Left: Negroni; bitter orange peel Florence, red Campari canals, moving gondolas made of gin ice]
[Bottom Right: Old Fashioned; bourbon barrel stave streets, sugar cube buildings, orange zest zeppelins]
Style: extreme macro cocktail photography, dramatic rim lighting, condensation, dark bar background, ultra-realistic
```

### No. 59: 2x2 Collage with Strict Identity and Pose Matching

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, structured JSON prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro designed for generating a 2x2 collage of a female subject, requiring strict preservation of facial identity, pose, camera angle, and expression based on an uploaded reference image. It details specific views (front, back, mirror selfie, side portrait) and environment settings (vintage-style indoor room) while locking the subject's identity and matching the reference image exactly.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "reference": {
      "face_identity": "uploaded reference image",
      "identity_lock": true,
      "pose_lock": true,
      "camera_angle_lock": true,
      "expression_lock": true,
      "face_preservation": "100% identical facial structure, proportions, eyes, lips, nose, brows, skin texture"
    },

    "composition": {
      "layout": "2x2 collage",
      "aspect_ratio": "1:1",
      "pose_matching": "exactly match reference image poses, angles, framing, and body orientation",
      "no_variation_allowed": true
    },

    "panel_1": {
      "view": "front-facing portrait",
      "pose": "head slightly tilted, eyes toward camera, soft lips",
      "framing": "chest-up selfie angle",
      "expression": "calm, elegant",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "panel_2": {
      "view": "back view",
      "pose": "standing facing mirror, arms raised slightly",
      "focus": "back of head and bow hairstyle",
      "framing": "upper-body rear shot",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "panel_3": {
      "view": "mirror selfie",
      "pose": "phone covering part of face, body angled sideways",
      "framing": "waist-up",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "panel_4": {
      "view": "side portrait",
      "pose": "head turned over shoulder looking into camera, holding bouquet close to chest",
      "expression": "soft romantic gaze",
      "framing": "upper torso",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "subject": {
      "gender": "female",
      "ethnicity": "Asian",
      "skin_tone": "fair with soft blush"
    },

    "hair": {
      "style": "long straight hair, half-up",
      "accessory": "large cream ribbon bow",
      "placement": "exact position as reference image"
    },

    "outfit": {
      "dress": {
        "color": "white",
        "pattern": "blue floral print",
        "style": "vintage puff-sleeve dress",
        "neckline": "square neckline"
      },
      "jewelry": [
        "pearl necklace",
        "delicate gold pendant"
      ]
    },

    "environment": {
      "location": "vintage-style indoor room",
      "background": [
        "ornate mirror",
        "cream walls",
        "soft floral decor",
        "classic furniture"
      ],
      "match_reference_background": true
    },

    "lighting": {
      "type": "soft indoor daylight",
      "quality": "even, gentle, warm",
      "shadow": "minimal",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "photography_style": {
      "style": "romantic vintage lifestyle",
      "lens": "DSLR portrait lens",
      "depth_of_field": "shallow",
      "color_grading": "soft pastel"
    },

    "render_quality": {
      "realism": "photorealistic",
      "resolution": "high",
      "texture_detail": "natural skin and fabric detail",
      "no_cartoon": true
    }
}
```

### No. 60: New Yorker Cartoon Style PPT Illustration Prompt

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A structured prompt designed for Nano Banana Pro to generate illustrations in the style of a New Yorker cartoonist, suitable for accompanying presentation slides (PPT). It specifies visual elements like pen and ink sketches, minimal backgrounds, metaphorical expression, and a high-contrast, limited color palette.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Generate accompanying illustrations similar to a New Yorker columnist cartoonist based on the content.
 
## Unified Visual Style

* **2K Clear Image**
* **Cartoon Illustration Texture:** Pen and ink sketch/hand-drawn lines, simple white space background
* **Metaphorical Expression:** Use visual language to convey deep meaning
* **Exquisite Details:** Relaxed line art, visually appealing
* **High-End Color Palette:** Primarily black and white, accented with a single color ({argument name="accent color" default="vermilion #E34234"}), minimalist elegance
* **Ink Rendering/Embellishment:** Enhances layering
* **Bottom Title:** Serif font, concise and powerful, Chinese

## Design Philosophy

* Tell stories using visual metaphors
* Simple but not simplistic, humorous but not shallow
* Every page is a work of art, worth savoring
* All pages maintain a unified style, color scheme, and texture
```

</div>

The silhouette is filled with a dense, ancient forest â€” towering trees, tangled branches, twisting roots, layered foliage â€” rendered in hand-sketched ink and blueprint-style linework. Mostly monochrome palette with selective {argument name="accent color" default="metallic gold"} accents catching light through leaves. #### ğŸ“– Description

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Turn a monumental structure into a functional piece of desk art.
 STEP 1:  Input image of a famous landmark 
 STEP 2: Scale down by 50,000%. Analyze its shape, geometry, color, material, unique characteristics.  
 STEP 3: Design a set of 9 next level clever gadgets and high tech home appliances inspired by the image
> OUTPUT: HIGH-FIDELITY IMAGEs. a 3x3 grid, each panel shallow-depth-of-field product photograph of a different object on an oak desk. It must look expensive. In the background,  relevant background, name underneath,
```

### No. 68: 8K Close-up Portrait of Indie Musician Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON prompt for generating a hyper-realistic, 8K close-up portrait of a young man with an indie musician vibe, emphasizing dramatic chiaroscuro lighting, a specific knit sweater pattern, and an 85mm lens emulation.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_generation_parameters": {
    "subject": {
      "identity": "Young man, Middle Eastern or South Asian descent",
      "features": [
        "Dark, thick, messy wavy hair",
        "Neatly groomed short beard and mustache",
        "Deep brown, intense eyes",
        "Direct gaze at camera"
      ],
      "pose": "Leaning forward, chin resting on crossed arms",
      "clothing": "Heavyweight, oversized 90s-style multi-colored Coogi-inspired knit sweater with 3D patchwork textures"
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "Dark studio",
      "background": "Mottled charcoal grey, textured plaster wall",
      "props": "Vintage black guitar amplifier with silver corner protectors and mesh grille"
    },
    "composition_and_lighting": {
      "shot_type": "Close-up portrait",
      "camera_angle": "Eye level",
      "lighting_style": "Dramatic Chiaroscuro, low-key lighting, soft highlights on hair and sweater texture",
      "focus": "Sharp focus on eyes, shallow depth of field (bokeh background)"
    },
    "technical_specs": {
      "lens_emulation": "85mm f/1.8",
      "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
      "style": "Hyper-realistic photography",
      "quality": "8k, high-fidelity textures, cinematic"
    },
    "keywords": [
      "indie musician vibe",
      "analog photography look",
      "moody atmosphere",
      "intricate knitwear patterns",
      "gritty elegance"
    ]
  }
}
```

### No. 69: Detailed Backstage Mirror Selfie Analysis Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured JSON prompt for Nano Banana Pro designed to generate a realistic, candid, backstage mirror selfie. The prompt includes extensive metadata, composition rules, a detailed color profile analysis, specific lighting parameters (hard light, high contrast, vanity lights), technical specs (digital noise, deep DOF), and artistic elements (K-pop idol aesthetic, Y2K fashion).

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
"metadata": {
"confidence_score": "high",
"image_type": "photograph",
"primary_purpose": "social media/behind-the-scenes/candid"
},
"composition": {
"rule_applied": "center composition",
"aspect_ratio": "3:4 vertical",
"layout": "single subject",
"focal_points": [
"Subject's face and upper torso",
"Smartphone with polka dot case"
],
"visual_hierarchy": "Eye is drawn to the subject's face, then moves to the phone case, down the torso to the outfit details, and finally scans the cluttered backstage environment.",
"balance": "asymmetric - heavy black negative space on left, cluttered details on right, subject centered"
},
"color_profile": {
"dominant_colors": [
{
"color": "Rust white",
"hex": "#8A5A4A",
"percentage": "15%",
"role": "subject clothing (top)"
},
{
"color": "Matte Black",
"hex": "#151515",
"percentage": "45%",
"role": "background curtains/phone/skirt"
},
{
"color": "Pale Porcelain Skin",
"hex": "#F3E2D5",
"percentage": "20%",
"role": "primary subject"
},
{
"color": "Platinum Blonde",
"hex": "#E6D6B8",
"percentage": "15%",
"role": "hair"
},
{
"color": "Plywood Beige",
"hex": "#A89F91",
"percentage": "5%",
"role": "ceiling structure"
}
],
"color_palette": "neutral with warm accents (brown/blonde vs black)",
"temperature": "mixed - cool blacks vs warm artificial lighting on skin",
"saturation": "moderate",
"contrast": "high contrast (bright subject vs dark background)"
},
"lighting": {
"type": "artificial/backstage vanity lights",
"source_count": "multiple sources (likely a vanity mirror array)",
"direction": "front",
"directionality": "moderately directional",
"quality": "hard light",
"intensity": "bright",
"contrast_ratio": "high contrast",
"mood": "raw/candid/backstage/edgy",
"shadows": {
"type": "harsh defined edges",
"density": "deep black",
"placement": "behind subject on the black curtain",
"length": "short"
},
"highlights": {
"treatment": "specular",
"placement": "forehead, nose bridge, collarbones, shoulders, cheekbones"
},
"ambient_fill": "minimal - falloff is rapid",
"light_temperature": "neutral/slightly cool white"
},
"technical_specs": {
"medium": "digital photography (smartphone mirror selfie)",
"style": "realistic/candid/snapshot",
"texture": "slightly grainy/digital noise visible",
"sharpness": "moderately sharp",
"grain": "digital noise (ISO grain visible in darks)",
"depth_of_field": "deep - everything relatively in focus due to wide lens and small sensor",
"perspective": "eye level/mirror reflection"
},
"artistic_elements": {
"genre": "selfie/celebrity style/behind-the-scenes",
"influences": [
"K-pop idol aesthetic",
"Y2K revival fashion",
"Casual instagram stories"
],
"mood": "cool/nonchalant/confident/rushed",
"atmosphere": "Backstage chaos, pre-performance prep, raw documentation",
"visual_style": "cluttered/authentic/flash-aesthetic"
},
"typography": {
"present": true,
"fonts": [
{
"type": "sans-serif",
"wei"
```

### No. 70: High-Contrast Monochrome Triptych Portrait with Steampunk Sunglasses

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON prompt for generating a hyper-realistic, 8k, monochrome triptych (3-panel photo grid) of a handsome man. It specifies the subject's clothing (black leather jacket, vintage steampunk aviator sunglasses), dramatic studio lighting, and requires three distinct angles and poses (frontal, profile, tilted head) while mandating the use of a reference face ID for consistency.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
Handsome man [Reference Face ID: 1.0]",
    "clothing": "Black leather jacket, vintage aviator sunglasses with leather side-shields (steampunk style)",
    "medium": "8k hyper-realistic photography, monochrome, black and white film",
    "layout": "Triptych, 3-panel photo grid, collage style, split screen",
    "action": "Three different angles and poses (frontal, profile, looking up), distinct expressions in each panel",
    "lighting": "Dramatic studio lighting, high contrast, rim lighting on leather texture",
    "full_prompt": "A high-contrast black and white triptych collage consisting of 3 distinct panels. A hyper-realistic 8k close-up portrait of a handsome man wearing a black leather jacket and vintage steampunk aviator sunglasses with leather side-shields. Panel 1: Front facing. Panel 2: Side profile. Panel 3: Tilted head. Detailed skin texture, pores visible, masculine features, cinematic lighting, photorealistic."
  },
  "negative_prompt": "color, polychromatic, cartoon, painting, sketch, 3d render, blurry, distorted, duplicate poses, same angle, bad anatomy, deformed, watermark, text, low quality, noise",
  "technical_settings": {
    "aspect_ratio": "16:9",
    "steps": 30,
    "guidance_scale": 7.5,
    "face_restoration": true,
    "notes": "Use ControlNet or IP-Adapter with the uploaded reference image to ensure 100% face consistency."
  }
}
```

### No. 71: Figure Product Introduction Layout Prompt (Japanese)

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed, structured prompt for Nano Banana Pro (Japanese only) designed to transform a reference image character into a photorealistic 1/7 scale PVC figure product introduction layout. It includes placeholders for product name and manufacturer, and specifies complex layout elements like multiple close-up panels, inferred pricing, material, and size information, all presented with Japanese text.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
product_name: "{argument name="product name" default="ARBITRARY_PRODUCT_NAME"}"
manufacturer_name: "{argument name="manufacturer name" default="ARBITRARY_MANUFACTURER_NAME"}"

subject: >
  The character from reference image A, faithfully preserved in design, proportions,
  facial features, hairstyle, outfit details, and color palette.
  The character is transformed into a highly detailed, photorealistic PVC figure.
  Sculpting style and overall aesthetic are inferred directly from the reference image.
  The figure is presented as a 1/7 scale collectible.

composition: >
  Japanese-language product introduction layout inferred by the model.
  Vertical composition with a 3:4 aspect ratio.
  A large main visual of the full figure.
  A single, clearly defined product information area containing all textual elements.
  Product name logo and manufacturer name logo are each displayed exactly once.
  Multiple inset close-up panels are included.
  Each inset must focus on a different physical area or feature of the figure.
  No two inset panels may depict the same part or the same visual characteristic.
  Inset panels must be visually and conceptually distinct from one another.

action: >
  Static collectible figure pose with no movement.
  Emphasis on sculpt accuracy, proportions, and surface detail.

location: >
  Neutral studio-like environment inferred for product photography.
  Minimal, non-distracting background.

style: >
  Photorealistic product rendering and photography style.
  Artistic tone and mood inferred entirely from the reference image.

camera_lighting: >
  Camera angle and lighting inferred for clear presentation of a collectible figure.
  Realistic studio lighting interacting with PVC surfaces.
  Glossy highlights on hair and clothing.
  Matte finish on skin.
  Sharp focus with natural depth of field.
  Soft shadow beneath the figure as if placed on a flat surface.

colors: >
  Exact color reproduction based on the reference image.
  Background and graphic elements inferred to support readability of Japanese text.

text: >
  Product Name:
  ã€Œ{{product_name}}ã€
  â€» The product name must be displayed and shown as a logo only once.

  Manufacturer Name:
  ã€Œ{{manufacturer_name}}ã€
  â€» The manufacturer name must also be displayed and shown as a logo only once.

  Scale:
  1/7 Scale Figure

  Sculptor:
  {{manufacturer_name}}

  Price:
  The inferred retail price in Japanese Yen, based on the figure's scale, sculpting density, and paint expression.

  Size:
  The inferred overall height in centimeters, based on the character's body type and the 1/7 scale setting.

  Material:
  Appropriate material for a figure.
```

### No. 72: Photorealistic Fashion Portrait on Car Hood at Seaside

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed, structured image generation prompt for creating a highly photorealistic outdoor fashion portrait. The prompt specifies maintaining the exact identity of a reference face while changing the outfit and environment to a cool, melancholic seaside setting with overcast lighting, featuring the subject sitting on the hood of a black sports car.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "reference_image": "use_uploaded_photo",
    "face_preservation": {
      "enabled": true,
      "strength": "maximum",
      "instruction": "Do not alter facial structure, proportions, skin texture, expression, moles, or identity in any way. The face must match the reference image exactly."
    },

    "subject": {
      "description": "A very beautiful young woman",
      "expression": "calm, slightly dreamy",
      "gaze": "looking directly at the camera",
      "skin": "natural, realistic skin texture",
      "makeup": {
        "style": "minimal with soft smokey eye makeup",
        "focus": "eyes subtly emphasized"
      },
      "hair": {
        "color": "dark brown",
        "length": "long",
        "style": "loose, wavy, slightly messy",
        "details": "a few strands partially covering her face for a natural, effortless look"
      }
    },

    "outfit_and_accessories": {
      "top": {
        "type": "loose white open shirt button",
        "fit": "relaxed",
        "details": "sleeves slightly rolled up at the wrists"
      },
      "outerwear": {
        "type": "formal black blazer",
        "placement": "draped over her left shoulder and resting slightly on the hood of the car"
      },
      "bottom": {
        "type": "dark pants",
        "color": "black",
        "visibility": "only partially visible"
      },
      "jewelry": {
        "neck": "layered chunky silver chain necklaces",
        "ears": "small silver hoop earrings",
        "wrist": "silver chain bracelet"
      }
    },

    "pose_and_composition": {
      "pose": "sitting casually on the hood of a car",
      "support": "leaning slightly back against the hood",
      "framing": "medium close-up",
      "focus": "sharp focus on the subject",
      "background_blur": "slight natural bokeh"
    },

    "environment": {
      "foreground": "glossy black sports car hood with subtle reflections",
      "background": {
        "location": "beach or seaside",
        "details": [
          "faint sandy shoreline",
          "calm grayish-blue ocean",
          "overcast or heavily cloudy sky"
        ],
        "atmosphere": "cool, melancholic, serene"
      }
    },

    "lighting": {
      "type": "soft natural daylight",
      "condition": "overcast",
      "effect": "evenly diffused lighting with no harsh shadows"
    },

    "photography_style": {
      "genre": "outdoor fashion portrait",
      "realism": "highly photorealistic",
      "color_tone": "cool and muted",
      "depth_of_field": "moderate with gentle background blur"
    },

    "quality": {
      "resolution": "ultra high",
      "detail": "sharp fabric, hair, jewelry, and skin textures",
      "render_style": "natural DSLR photography look"
    }
  }
}
```

### No. 75: Vibrant Jet Ski Selfie with Strict Identity Lock

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro, designed to generate a vibrant, photorealistic action portrait of a woman riding a jet ski. The prompt enforces a strict identity lock based on a reference image, ensuring the facial features, skin texture, and hair type remain 100% faithful to the source, while placing the subject in an open ocean setting with bright natural sunlight.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "type": "image_generation_prompt",
  "style": "realistic, vibrant, photorealistic action portrait",
  "identity_preservation": {
    "use_reference_image": true,
    "alter_face": false,
    "strict_identity_lock": true,
    "notes": "Use the attached reference image as a strict source. Keep the womanâ€™s facial features, facial structure, skin texture, hair type, and accessories exactly the same with 100% fidelity."
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "female",
    "pose": {
      "activity": "riding a jet ski",
      "camera_angle": "selfie angle",
      "framing": "head and chest visible",
      "expression": "natural, relaxed, adventurous"
    },
    "appearance": {
      "hair": {
        "color": "dark",
        "style": "natural",
        "notes": "No long hair, no sunglasses"
      }
    },
    "wardrobe": {
      "life_jacket": "black life jacket"
    }
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "open ocean",
    "water": "slightly rippled ocean surface",
    "sky": {
      "condition": "clear blue sky",
      "lighting": "bright natural sunlight"
    },
    "background": {
      "elements": [
        "other people riding jet skis in the distance"
      ],
      "focus": "softly blurred to create depth and motion"
    }
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "natural daylight",
    "quality": "bright, clean, and realistic",
    "effects": [
      "natural highlights on skin and water",
      "sense of motion and energy"
    ]
  },
  "camera": {
    "look": "selfie action shot",
    "focus": "sharp focus on face and upper body",
    "movement": "slight motion feel from riding",
    "quality": "high clarity and sharpness"
  },
  "mood": {
    "atmosphere": "lively, adventurous, energetic",
    "tone": "fresh, fun, and dynamic"
  },
  "quality": {
    "realism": "highly photorealistic",
    "detail_level": "sharp details in face, water, and lighting",
    "color_accuracy": "natural colors, no artificial tones"
  },
  "negative_prompt": [
    "blurry face",
    "distorted proportions",
    "unrealistic lighting",
    "deformed hands",
    "wrong facial structure",
    "incorrect accessories",
    "extra people in the foreground",
    "disfigured body",
    "cartoon style",
    "painting",
    "artificial colors",
    "low quality",
    "watermark",
    "text",
    "long hair"
  ],
  "output_goal": "Create a realistic, vibrant, and energetic selfie-style ocean portrait of a woman riding a jet ski, preserving her exact facial identity while conveying motion, sunlight, and adventure."
}
```

### No. 76: Kawaii Gamer Cosplay Mirror Selfie Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON prompt, structured with meta and engine configuration, for generating a mirror selfie photograph of a young woman in a kawaii gamer cosplay aesthetic (cow ears, cow-print top) in a bedroom with RGB lighting.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "meta": {
    "project": "Kawaii_Gamer_Public_Demo",
```

### No. 80: Detailed Mirror Selfie Image Analysis Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A structured prompt designed to analyze and replicate a mirror selfie image, detailing the subject's appearance, outfit (faux fur jacket, black corset top, low-rise jeans), accessories, pose, and specific lighting conditions.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_analysis_prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "demographics": "Young woman",
      "hair": {
        "color": "Strawberry blonde / Golden blonde",
        "style": "Long, voluminous, layered, slightly messy waves",
        "parting": "Middle part"
      },
      "face": {
        "makeup": "Winged black eyeliner, mascara, defined eyebrows, highlighter on nose and cheeks, glossy pink lips",
        "expression": "Neutral to slight pout, focused on mirror reflection"
      },
      "physique": "Slender, fit, tan skin tone"
    },
    "apparel": {
      "outerwear": {
        "item": "Faux fur jacket",
        "color": "Brown/Taupe mixed tones",
        "texture": "Shaggy, plush, voluminous"
      },
      "top": {
        "item": "Corset top",
        "style": "Strapless, bustier-style, cropped",
        "material": "Black satin or slightly shiny fabric",
        "fit": "Tight, structured bodice"
      },
      "bottoms": {
        "item": "Jeans",
        "color": "Light blue wash",
        "fit": "Low-rise, tight fit",
        "details": "Visible stitching, front pockets"
      }
    },
    "accessories": {
      "jewelry": [
        "Thin gold chain necklace with small pendant",
        "Gold ring on right ring finger"
      ],
      "belt": {
        "material": "Black leather",
        "buckle": "Rectangular gold/metallic frame"
      },
      "tech": {
        "item": "Smartphone (iPhone style)",
        "case_color": "Black",
        "holding_style": "Held vertically in front of face with right hand"
      },
      "beauty_details": {
        "nails": "Short, painted bright red"
      }
    },
    "pose_and_framing": {
      "type": "Mirror selfie",
      "posture": "Standing, slight hip tilt (contrapposto), midriff exposed",
      "framing": "Thigh-up shot, portrait orientation"
    },
    "setting_and_lighting": {
      "location": "Indoors (likely a bedroom or hallway)",
      "background_elements": {
        "left": "Dark window with blinds, glimpse of bed/furniture with white clutter",
        "right": "White door frame/jamb, plain wall"
      },
      "lighting": {
        "quality": "Warm, directional artificial light",
        "source": "Coming from the right side",
        "shadows": "Casts shadows on the left side of the torso and background"
      }
    }
  }
}
```

### No. 83: AKIRA 'Slide Brake Scene' Recreation Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly specific, multi-section prompt for Nano Banana Pro designed to recreate the iconic 'slide brake scene' from the anime AKIRA, without using the word 'AKIRA'. It details composition, subject, action, visual effects (smoke trails, neon-green energy arcs), and art style (1980s cyberpunk anime aesthetic).

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
(VARIABLE SCENE - EDIT HERE):
Nighttime, expansive {argument name="cityscape" default="Neo-Tokyo"} highway. Futuristic cityscape background with neon lights.
Strong one-point perspective: The road stretches straight from the bottom edge to the vanishing point in the center.

(CRITICAL COMPOSITION):
One-point perspective composition with the subject in the CENTER.
Subject Orientation: The motorcycle is shown in SIDE PROFILE (facing Screen Left).
TILT ANGLE: The motorcycle body is LEANING HEAVILY TOWARDS THE CAMERA (The top of the bike is closer to the viewer than the wheels).
Movement direction: The bike is sliding away from the camera, moving from the foreground deep into the background.
Placement: Bike is perfectly centered in the frame.

(SUBJECT):
A futuristic motorcycle and rider.
Motorcycle:
- Heavy, solid, rounded silhouette
- Minimal exposed mechanics, smooth cowling
- Wide, thick, high-grip tires
- Color scheme harmonized with rider
Rider:
- Face and outfit preserved from reference image
- Stare straight into the camera, glaring with a powerful, piercing gaze.
- Left foot planted firmly on the ground, struggling to support the heavy leaning bike
- Rider's leg is fully extended to brace against the fall

(ACTION & MECHANICS):
High-speed linear slide braking (NOT cornering).
The bike is sliding sideways while traveling backwards into the depth of the scene.
Instability: The bike is on the verge of falling over towards the screen.
Wheels are locked (not rotating).

(VISUAL EFFECTS - SMOKE TRAILS):
Three distinct, straight trails of thick white smoke.
Direction: Smoke stretches from the IMMEDIATE FOREGROUND (bottom of screen) directly to the motorcycle's wheels and rider's foot in the center.
The smoke trails act as leading lines pointing to the subject.
Violent debris and asphalt fragments kicking up.

(ENERGY EFFECTS):
Neon-green lightning energy arcs (1980s anime style) embedded within the white smoke trails.
Green energy flows through the smoke, following the straight lines from foreground to the bike.

(ART STYLE):
Cel-shaded animation, 1980s anime aesthetic (Cyberpunk).
High contrast, bold black shadows, dramatic lighting.
Poster-quality, ultra-high resolution, sharp focus.
```

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly specific JSON prompt for generating a photorealistic full-body mirror selfie of a young woman in a modern gym, emphasizing identity lock to match an uploaded reference image exactly, down to facial structure and skin texture, while detailing her outfit and the gym environment.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "reference": {
      "face_identity": "use uploaded reference image",
      "identity_lock": true,
      "face_accuracy": "100% identical to reference â€” same facial structure, proportions, skin texture, expression, and details"
    },

    "subject": {
      "type": "young woman",
      "appearance": {
        "hair": {
          "color": "dark brown",
          "style": "long wavy hair with a half-up messy bun, loose strands framing the face"
        },
        "skin": {
          "tone": "same as reference image",
          "texture": "natural, realistic"
        },
        "expression": "calm, composed, slightly focused",
        "gaze": "looking at phone screen"
      },
      "pose": {
        "stance": "standing with one leg slightly forward",
        "hands": {
          "right": "holding a black smartphone for a mirror selfie",
          "left": "holding a transparent water bottle with brown liquid"
        }
      }
    },

    "outfit": {
      "top": {
        "primary": "fitted white t-shirt",
        "layer": "white long-sleeve baggy hoddie"
      },
      "bottom": {
        "type": "joggers black",
        "color": "navy blue"
      },
      "footwear": {
        "shoes": "white athletic sneakers",
        "socks": "white crew socks"
      }
    },

    "environment": {
      "location": "modern indoor gym",
      "features": [
        "large wall mirrors",
        "treadmills",
        "weight machines",
        "rubber gym flooring",
        "exercise mats on the floor"
      ],
      "reflection": "mirror seam visible vertically in frame"
    },

    "lighting": {
      "type": "bright overhead fluorescent gym lighting",
      "quality": "even, neutral illumination with minimal shadows"
    },

    "composition": {
      "shot_type": "full-body mirror selfie",
      "camera_angle": "eye-level",
      "framing": "centered subject",
      "style": "casual fitness lifestyle photograph"
    },

    "image_style": {
      "realism": "highly photorealistic",
      "detail": "sharp clothing textures and clear gym background",
      "mood": "clean, modern, casual",
      "resolution": "high resolution"
    }
  }
}
```

### No. 89: Fine Art Low-Key Portrait in Vintage Dress

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed prompt for Nano Banana Pro requesting a realistic fine art studio portrait of a young woman (based on a reference photo) in a semi-side pose, wearing a vintage-romantic ivory dress, emphasizing cinematic low-key lighting and a mysterious, confident expression.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A realistic fine art studio portrait of a slim young woman (face identical to the attached reference photo) with pale skin and naturally dark, curly hair at shoulder length. She is lying on a soft surface in a semi-side pose, her body placed diagonally within the frame. One arm is bent and placed behind her head, while the other arm is gently raised with a relaxed wrist and graceful fingers. Her legs are softly bent, creating flowing, elegant body lines. Her head faces straight toward the camera with her chin slightly lifted.

Her facial expression is calm, confident, and subtly mysterious. Her gaze looks directly into the camera, with naturally thick eyebrows. Her lips are warm red with soft, classic makeup. There is no smile, giving a strong yet poetic impression.

She wears an ivory white vintageâ€“romantic style dress with short puff sleeves, featuring delicate lace and fine embroidery details on the bodice. The satin or silk fabric appears soft and drapes naturally along her body with gentle folds. The fabric texture is clearly visible yet smooth.

Lighting: Soft, cinematic low-key lighting. A single diffused light source from the sideâ€“top direction softly illuminates the face, chest, and folds of the dress. Gentle highlights create a glowing effect on the fabric and skin, while deep yet smooth shadows envelop the sides of the body and background. No harsh light. Medium contrast with very smooth shadow transitions, creating an intimate and classic atmosphere.

Background: A plain dark cushioned background in deep greenish-black, without details, with a natural vignette around the edges of the frame to enhance focus on the subject.

Visual style: Fine art portrait photography, vintage cinematic, painterly realism, romantic gothic, old master inspired, classic and dramatic yet soft mood.

Technical details: Shallow depth of field, sharp focus on the face, clear fabric details, slight soft focus, fine grain, cinematic color grading, muted colors, high quality, no excessive modern effects.

Negative Prompt: stiff pose, harsh lighting, overly bright colors, HDR, ultra sharp, modern style, modern clothing, busy background, modern makeup.
```

### No. 90: Glamorous Fashion Portrait in Pink Chiffon Dress

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed prompt for generating an ultra-realistic, editorial fashion photograph of a woman in a dramatic pink lace and chiffon high-low dress, set in a grand foyer with dramatic backlighting from a stained-glass window, focusing on texture quality and sophisticated atmosphere.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "prompt_description": {
    "subject": "A young adult woman with a slender, athletic build, likely in her early to mid-twenties.",
    "face": "A delicate face with high cheekbones and a strong jawline. Her eyes are large and dark, with a subtle, alluring gaze directed slightly past the viewer. Her lips are full and slightly parted, hinting at a gentle smile. Her skin is smooth with minimal visible texture, suggesting a soft, airbrushed appearance.",
    "hair": "Long, dark brown hair with a natural wave. It's styled to fall over one shoulder, with loose strands framing her face. The texture appears silky and healthy, with subtle highlights catching the light.",
    "clothing": "A two-piece ensemble. The top is a strapless bodice with intricate pink lace detailing and embellishments around the bust. A thin, shimmering band cinches the waist. The skirt is a dramatic, high-low design made of layered, sheer pink chiffon. The layers are asymmetrical and ruffled, creating a voluminous and flowing effect. The hemline is significantly shorter in the front, revealing her legs, and cascades into a longer train at the back. The fabric of the skirt appears lightweight and ethereal, with delicate folds and drapes. The top is form-fitting, while the skirt has a relaxed yet structured flow.",
    "accessories": "Sparkling, pointed-toe high heels adorned with glitter or sequins, featuring a delicate ankle strap. Subtle stud earrings.",
    "environment": "Indoors, in what appears to be a grand foyer or ballroom. The background is dominated by a large, arched window with decorative stained-glass panels. Tall, elegant white molding and columns suggest a classical architectural style. Lush green foliage is visible through the window, indicating an outdoor garden or park setting. Sunlight streams through the window, creating a dappled light effect on the floor.",
    "lighting": "Dramatic backlighting from the large window, casting a soft glow on the subject and creating rim lighting around her hair and silhouette. The light is diffused by the window panes and foliage, creating soft shadows. There. are warm specular highlights on her skin, the fabric of her dress, and her shoes. The overall lighting creates a sense of depth and dimension.",
    "atmosphere": "Elegant, sophisticated, and subtly sensual. The mood is aspirational and glamorous, evoking a sense of special occasion and refined beauty."
  },
  "style": {
    "art_style": "Ultra-realistic commercial photography, editorial fashion",
    "color_grade": "Warm, soft color grading with an emphasis on pastel pinks and muted golden tones from the sunlight. Shadows have a slight cool cast from the ambient interior light.",
    "texture_quality": "Extremely high detail and sharpness, with micro-contrast that emphasizes the textures of the fabric, lace, and sequins. Skin texture is smooth and refined. Realistic rendering of light interaction with materials."
```

```
Photorealistic kitchen at dawn. Single light source from a small east-facing window. Stainless steel sink with three water droplets only, no more. One green apple with a visible bruise. Wooden table with a shallow scratch shaped like a crescent. No people. Natural color science. 50mm lens look. Zero stylization
```

### No. 93: Tang Dynasty Empress in Paris Fashion Magazine Cover Prompt

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extremely detailed, multi-section prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate a 9:16 vertical, realistic fashion magazine cover photo. The subject, whose facial features must be 100% consistent with a reference image, is dressed in opulent Tang Dynasty court attire (Qixiong Shanqun, large sleeves, peony patterns, gold ornaments) and photographed against the backdrop of the Eiffel Tower in Paris. The prompt specifies lighting, color matrix (Tang Dynasty colors), pose (confident Empress), and magazine-level composition.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Generate a 9:16 vertical, realistic photo of 'Prosperous Tang Dynasty meets Paris': Use the uploaded FACE_REF as the character identity reference, 100% restoring the facial features and bone structure; the character is wearing a heavy-duty court gown in the style of a 'Tang Dynasty (High Tang) Imperial Concubine' (Qixiong Shanqun, large sleeves, peony patterns, gold ornaments), photographed at TrocadÃ©ro Square or the banks of the Seine beneath the Eiffel Tower in Paris. The image should have the photography, styling, and cover design quality of a COSMO fashion magazine, maintaining the magazine's consistent design style (English design).

ã€INPUTS | Inputã€‘ FACE_REF: The uploaded reference image for the character's facial features (Identity Lock)

ã€ABSOLUTE PRIORITY | Identity Lock (Highest Priority)ã€‘ 100% restoration of FACE_REF's facial features and bone structure: Face shape, appearance, eye distance, nose bridge/alae, lip shape, jawline, and cheekbone structure must be completely consistent, without drifting. Realistic skin texture: Visible subtle textures and pores, avoid excessive smoothing or 'influencer' style. Adult female image.

ã€SHOT TYPE | Choose one of two shots (randomly selected by the model, must be truly consistent)ã€‘ A) Bust Cover: From the chest to above the waist, the headwear and upper body embroidery are clearest, eyes are sharpest focus (Primary recommendation) B) Full Body Cover: Complete presentation of the layered gown and skirt patterns from head to toe, stronger perspective of the Eiffel Tower's steel structure (Alternative) (Regardless of A/B: must maintain 'cover composition', with white space for layout, but no torn paper/hand-drawn effects.)

ã€LOCATION | Scene (Eiffel Tower, Paris)ã€‘ Eiffel Tower, Paris: Classic steel structure tower background. Choose one of two weather conditions (random): 1) Rainy Paris (ground slightly wet, soft light, high-end gray tone, strong fashion sense) 2) Brilliant Dusk (sunset glow, golden light and shadow, romantic atmosphere) Clean background: No tourists, no modern signs, no phone status bar UI, no watermarks/subtitles, no railings.

ã€LIGHTING & CAMERA | Photography Quality (Magazine Level)ã€‘ Lens feel: 85mm portrait quality (bust) or 50mm/70mm (full body), shallow depth of field, eyes in sharpest focus. Lighting: Natural light (emphasizing ambient light) + cinematic fill light; gold ornaments have realistic highlights but are not blown out; silk luster is clearly discernible. Color: High-end cinematic feel, French beige/blue-gray tones form a strong visual tension with the Tang Dynasty clothing's 'red, green, and gold' color scheme; overall clean, transparent, and rich in texture.

ã€WARDROBE | Tang Dynasty Court Gown (Plump, Flowing, Intense Colors)ã€‘ Target aesthetic: 'Ornate gold ornaments, facial makeup (mianye huadian), Qixiong skirt, flowing pibo (long scarf), intense red, green, and gold, extremely flamboyant.'

Silhouette and Layers (Must reflect Tang Dynasty characteristics) Inner layer: Hezi (bustier), exposing the neck and upper chest skin (reflecting the open atmosphere of the Tang Dynasty) Middle layer: Duijin short jacket (straight collar), transparent and light material (gauze/silk) Outer layer: Daxiu Shan (extremely wide sleeves, dragging on the floor), spread out like wings Decoration: Pibo (long silk ribbon), wrapped around the arms, fluttering in the wind Bottom wear: Qixiong Poqun (skirt waist tied at the chest, wide skirt hem, multi-color splicing or printing) Fabric and Craftsmanship (Heavy craftsmanship must be 'visible') Main fabrics: Silk, brocade, gold-printed gauze (combination of lightness and heaviness) Main techniques: Printing and dyeing (wax resist/clamping), gold thread embroidery, gold weaving Pattern themes (suitable for High Tang): Baoxiang flower, continuous peony vine, auspicious beasts (lion/kylin), Tuanhua (giant, full patterns) Details: Huadian (red decoration on the forehead), Mianye (red dots at the corners of the mouth), Armband (metal ornament on the upper arm) Headwear (Opulent Tang Dynasty headwear) Core structure: High bun (Yunji/Zhuaimaji), adorned with large peony flowers (real or silk) Decoration: Gold comb back (gold comb inserted into the bun), Buyao (swaying when moving), gold hairpin Earrings: Precious gold and jade

ã€COLOR MATRIX | Color Matrix Pairing (Must be executed, and must be 'Intense Tang Style')ã€‘ (Adjusted to Tang Dynasty popular colors: red-green contrast, brilliant gold) Randomly select 1 set from the following three 'Main Color Schemes' for the [Base Color/Large Area Main Fabric Color].

Scheme G (Stone Blue/Emerald Green Base): Base Color: {argument name="base color 1" default="Emerald Green/Stone Blue"} (common intermediate color) Embroidery/Printing: Madder Red, Gold, Orange Yellow, Off-White Scheme A (Peony Red Base): Base Color: {argument name="base color 2" default="Peony Red/Pomegranate Red"} (most classic Tang style) Embroidery/Printing: Gold, Emerald Green, Sapphire Blue, Purple Scheme R (Purple Base): Base Color: {argument name="base color 3" default="Purple/Grape Color"} (noble) Embroidery/Printing: Gold, Vermilion, Grass Green, Silver

ã€Color Execution Rulesã€‘ Color contrast must be strong, reflecting the grandeur of the High Tang, but the overall tone must be unified in a high-end feel.

ã€POSE | Cover Pose (Confident, Expansive, Queenly Feel)ã€‘ Bust: Head slightly raised, eyes looking down, one hand gently touching the bun or pibo Full Body: Arms spread out to drive the Daxiu Shan and Pibo, showcasing the volume of the clothing, full aura Expression: Confident, flamboyant, charming, generous; not shy.

ã€OUTPUT | Outputã€‘ 1 vertical 9:16 realistic magazine cover-level photo Random: Bust or Full Body (A/B choice) Random: Rainy or Dusk (Weather choice) Random: Emerald Green / Peony Red / Purple (Color matrix choice) Styling: Tang Dynasty court gown direction + Peony flower/Gold comb headwear + Qixiong Daxiu + Pibo
```

### No. 94: Realistic Library Scene at Foggy Autumn Dawn

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt used for comparing multiple image models (GPT Image 1.5, Nano Banana Pro, Flux 2, Grok), describing a realistic scene inside a grand library during a foggy autumn dawn. The focus is on a South Asian woman sitting at a large wooden table, surrounded by ancient books, with muted sunlight struggling to penetrate the fog.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A realistic depiction of a grand library during a foggy autumn dawn. Muted sunlight struggles to penetrate the thick fog outside. A South Asian woman with black hair in a neat braid, wearing a grey cardigan over a white blouse and black skirt, sits at a large wooden table, surrounded by ancient books.
```

#### ğŸ–¼ï¸ Generated Images

```
A hyper-realistic medium portrait of a stunning {argument name="age" default="20-year-old"} woman sitting at a table in a cozy, dimly lit upscale restaurant, posing directly for the camera. She is wearing a chic, textured {argument name="sweater color" default="cream-colored"} cashmere sweater and a delicate gold necklace.

The lighting is cinematic and warm, utilizing the candlelight to create soft shadows on her face (Rembrandt lighting), highlighting natural skin texture, visible pores, and slight imperfections to ensure realism.
The background is a beautiful, creamy bokeh of the restaurant interior, featuring blurred warm hanging lights, brick walls, and faint silhouettes of other diners. Shot on a Sony A7R IV with an 85mm f/1.2 GM lens, depth of field, 8k resolution, raw photography style, highly detailed, photorealistic. --ar 1:1
```

### No. 105: Candid Morning Selfie with Elon Musk Polaroid

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt for generating an ultra-realistic, candid morning selfie with a specific, humorous element: the subject is seated on the floor in a messy bedroom, interacting with a large polaroid photograph of Elon Musk. It emphasizes the natural, unstyled mobile-camera feel and soft Scandinavian lighting.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "intent": "Generate an ultra-realistic, candid morning selfie with a relaxed, spontaneous atmosphere.",
  "frame": {
    "aspect_ratio": "9:16 vertical",
    "composition": "Low, close camera angle slightly from the side, focusing on the subjectâ€™s face and a large polaroid on the floor beneath her.",
    "style_mode": "photorealistic, cinematic-natural, authentic mobile-camera feel",
    "depth_of_field": "shallow, subject and polaroid in focus, background softly blurred"
  },
  "subject": {
    "identity": "use the reference face and body exactly",
    "pose": {
      "position": "Seated on the floor on a crumpled rug",
      "legs": "One knee bent, the other leg stretched out comfortably",
      "torso": "Leaning slightly forward, angled toward the camera",
      "head": "Tilted slightly downward with eyes looking up toward the camera"
    },
    "expression": "Curious, playful, candid morning expression with a relaxed demeanor",
    "hair": {
      "style": "Naturally tousled bed-hair, unstyled as if just woke up"
    },
    "wardrobe": {
      "top": "Oversized white sleep shirt worn loosely and comfortably",
      "bottom": "Simple lounge shorts",
      "overall": "Casual, non-stylized morning loungewear"
    },
    "interaction": {
      "object": "Large polaroid photograph of Elon Musk",
      "details": "The polaroid clearly shows a single portrait of Elon Musk and no one else, fully visible beneath the subject. One hand rests near the polaroid, lightly touching its edge."
    }
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "Messy bedroom",
    "background_elements": [
      "Unmade bed with twisted sheets and duvet",
      "Clothes scattered on a chair",
      "Open wardrobe door"
    ],
    "lighting": {
      "type": "Soft natural daylight",
      "source": "Side window",
      "quality": "Cool Scandinavian morning light with gentle shadows, no harsh contrast"
    }
  },
  "aesthetic": {
    "mood": "Intimate, relaxed, spontaneous",
    "color_grading": "Cinematic but natural",
    "detail": "High-resolution, photorealistic skin texture"
  },
  "priority_notes": [
    "Maintain clear visibility of the large Elon Musk polaroid beneath the subject",
    "Preserve a natural, unposed, morning snapshot feel",
    "Avoid exaggerated styling or dramatic lighting"
  ]
}
```

```
        "classic Parisian rooftops",
        "winding streets below"
      ],

    }

  },
  "mood": {
```

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

Bounty: Male alien humanoid criminal (tentacle beard, blue skin, restrained with glowing energy cuffs), disheveled prisoner outfit, defeated glare. Environment consistency: Gritty galactic outpost spaceport at duskâ€”dusty landing pads, neon-lit cantina signs in alien languages, hovering drones, distant starry sky with twin moons, scattered cargo crates, worn metal walkways, atmospheric haze with floating dust particles. Style: Cinematic sci-fi drama like Blade Runner meets The Mandalorian, highly detailed photorealistic rendering, dramatic volumetric lighting with neon blues/purples/oranges, lens flares from ship engines, subtle film grain, epic widescreen composition vibes. Grid layout and progression (top-left â†’ top-right â†’ bottom-left â†’ bottom-right): Panel 1 (wide establishing shot): Bounty hunter standing confidently in the outpost's dusty detention area, looking at a holographic bounty poster, alien bounty shows a menacing looking alien. Panel 2 (medium action shot): She walks with down the outpost, high-tech watch logs the bouny job just took, passersby (aliens and humans) glancing warily, hovering advertisement drones overhead. Panel 3 (three-quarter tracking shot): Hunter walking toward her parked sleek black bounty hunter spaceship (angular design with glowing engine vents), ramp lowering automatically as she approach, outpost towers and landing lights in background. Panel 4 (dynamic low-angle heroic shot): Inside the ship's cockpit from behindâ€”hunter strapping in at pilot controls, starting engines with holographic displays activating and thrusters glowing bright blue, bounty secured in rear holding cell visible through glass, ship beginning liftoff as outpost recedes below, stars ahead. Aspect ratio 1:1 for perfect square grid, ultra-detailed cinematic masterpiece, best quality, dramatic sci-fi lighting and atmosphere."

### No. 116: Structured JSON Prompt for Candid Mirror Selfie in a Bohemian Bedroom

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro to generate a candid mirror selfie photograph of a young woman in a dimly lit, cluttered, bohemian-style bedroom. The prompt specifies subject identity based on a reference image, hair style, clothing, pose (sitting cross-legged, holding a smartphone), environment details (vintage dresser, white metal stool), and a film-like photography style with grain and muted colors.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "detailed_prompts": {
    "subject_identity": [
      "A young woman, whose specific appearance and reddish-orange hair color are based on the reference image_19.png."
    ],
    "hair_style": [
      "Her reddish-orange hair is tied up into a messy, casual bun, similar to the style in image_19.png but less neat, with stray strands framing her face."
    ],
    "clothing": [
      "She is wearing a simple, light grey or faded blue t-shirt, similar in style to the one in image_22.png."
    ],
    "pose_and_action": [
      "She is sitting cross-legged on a bed, similar to the pose in image_19.png and image_22.png.",
      "She is holding a smartphone in front of her face with one hand, taking a mirror selfie, obscuring most of her face.",
      "Her other hand is resting on a crumpled white duvet."
    ],
    "environment_main": [
      "The setting is a dimly lit, bohemian-style bedroom, similar to the one in image_22.png.",
      "The room has a lived-in, cluttered, and cozy feel."
    ],
    "environment_furniture_and_objects": [
      "In the background, there is a vintage green-painted dresser with open drawers.",
      "On top of the dresser, there are various items like bottles, a small mirror, and personal objects.",
      "A white metal stool is visible near the dresser.",
      "A large mirror on the wall reflects the scene.",
      "A crumpled white duvet and blankets are on the bed."
    ],
    "lighting_details": [
      "The room is dimly lit with natural, soft light coming from a window (off-camera), creating a moody and intimate atmosphere, similar to the lighting in image_22.png.",
      "The lighting is not harsh but creates soft shadows."
    ],
    "Photography_style": [
      "A candid mirror selfie photograph.",
      "The photo has a film-like quality with visible grain, muted colors, and a slightly desaturated, warm tone, similar to the aesthetic of image.png."
    ]
  }
```

### No. 117: Multi-Cut Image Generation with Style Variation

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt designed to generate a single image containing a 3x3 grid of 9 cuts. All cuts feature the same person, composition, pose, and camera position, but each cut applies a different artistic style (e.g., cel anime, oil painting, photorealistic 3D) for comparison.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Based on the reference image, generate a multi-cut image with 9 cuts arranged within a single image.
The layout is a 3x3 uniform grid. Each cut features the same person, same composition, same pose, and same camera position.
Specify the style for each cut (from top left to bottom right):
Cel animation style (TV anime style, clean line art, 2-3 levels of shadow)
Movie anime style (delicate lines, rich gradient shadows)
Black and white manga style (ink lines, screen tones)
Watercolor illustration (paper texture, bleeding, pale colors)
Oil painting (thick application, brushstrokes, canvas feel)
High-quality 3D cartoon (soft modeling, subsurface scattering)
Photorealistic 3D (PBR, texture close to real life)
Claymation (clay texture, handmade feel)
Cyberpunk color grading (cyan/magenta rim light, background remains plain)
Ensure that all 9 cuts have completely identical composition, person, pose, and background, allowing only the style difference to be compared.
Arrange them naturally as one complete image.
```

### No. 119: Identity-Locked 2x2 Vintage Collage

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed, structured prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro, focusing on strict identity, pose, and composition locking to recreate a 2x2 collage of a subject (Asian female) in a vintage aesthetic, ensuring pixel-perfect matching across all elements based on a reference image.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "reference": {
      "face_identity": "uploaded reference image",
      "identity_lock": true,
      "pose_lock": true,
      "camera_angle_lock": true,
      "expression_lock": true,
      "face_preservation": "100% identical facial structure, proportions, eyes, lips, nose, brows, skin texture"
    },

    "composition": {
      "layout": "2x2 collage",
      "aspect_ratio": "1:1",
      "pose_matching": "exactly match reference image poses, angles, framing, and body orientation",
      "no_variation_allowed": true
    },

    "panel_1": {
      "view": "front-facing portrait",
      "pose": "head slightly tilted, eyes toward camera, soft lips",
      "framing": "chest-up selfie angle",
      "expression": "calm, elegant",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "panel_2": {
      "view": "back view",
      "pose": "standing facing mirror, arms raised slightly",
      "focus": "back of head and bow hairstyle",
      "framing": "upper-body rear shot",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "panel_3": {
      "view": "mirror selfie",
      "pose": "phone covering part of face, body angled sideways",
      "framing": "waist-up",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "panel_4": {
      "view": "side portrait",
      "pose": "head turned over shoulder looking into camera, holding bouquet close to chest",
      "expression": "soft romantic gaze",
      "framing": "upper torso",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "subject": {
      "gender": "female",
      "ethnicity": "Asian",
      "skin_tone": "fair with soft blush"
    },

    "hair": {
      "style": "long straight hair, half-up",
      "accessory": "large cream ribbon bow",
      "placement": "exact position as reference image"
    },

    "outfit": {
      "dress": {
        "color": "white",
        "pattern": "blue floral print",
        "style": "vintage puff-sleeve dress",
        "neckline": "square neckline"
      },
      "jewelry": [
        "pearl necklace",
        "delicate gold pendant"
      ]
    },

    "environment": {
      "location": "vintage-style indoor room",
      "background": [
        "ornate mirror",
        "cream walls",
        "soft floral decor",
        "classic furniture"
      ],
      "match_reference_background": true
    },

    "lighting": {
      "type": "soft indoor daylight",
      "quality": "even, gentle, warm",
      "shadow": "minimal",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "photography_style": {
      "style": "romantic vintage lifestyle",
      "lens": "DSLR portrait lens",
      "depth_of_field": "shallow",
      "color_grading": "soft pastel"
    },

    "render_quality": {
      "realism": "photorealistic",
      "resolution": "high",
      "texture_detail": "natural skin and fabric detail",
      "no_cartoon": true
    }
  }
}
```

### No. 120: Editorial Photography of Woman in Armchair with Sheep

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A JSON prompt specifying the visual elements, composition, and color palette for generating an editorial photograph. The scene features a woman in an armchair, set against a natural landscape background with sheep, utilizing warm golden hour lighting and deep depth of field.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "colors": {
    "palette": [
      "#4B4B4B",
      "#8B6C5C",
      "#D9D3C5",
      "#2B3A42",
      "#A59C84"
    ],
    "dominant_colors": {
      "foreground": "#D9D3C5",
      "background": "#A59C84",
      "accents": "#8B6C5C"
    }
  },
  "typography": null,
  "composition": {
    "layout": "Portrait",
    "focal_point": "Central subject (woman in armchair)",
    "framing": "Wide shot, full body view, natural landscape background",
    "depth_of_field": "Deep, with sharp focus on subject and mid-ground sheep, soft background mountains"
  },
  "effects": {
    "lighting": "Warm, golden hour sunlight, soft shadows",
    "atmosphere": "Pastoral, serene, natural, editorial photography",
    "texture": "Fabric of dress, leather of chair and boots, grass, wool of sheep"
  }
}
```

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-nano-banana-pro-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
